## Domain Knowledge
**Domain**: chemical reaction kinetics (rate laws and kinetic ODE models)
**Analysis**: The target dA_dt is an ODE for the time-derivative of a species concentration A, which is the standard setup for chemical kinetics. With only (t, A) available, the most common models are single-species rate laws (decay/production), possibly with time-varying or deactivation terms folded into explicit t-dependence.

**Common formula structures** (built-in generic + LLM domain-specific):
- Arrhenius equation: k = c0 * exp(c1 / T) (chemical reaction rate dependence on temperature)
- Coulomb's / Newton's inverse-square law: F = c0 / r**2 (gravitational or electrostatic force)
- Stefan-Boltzmann law: P = c0 * T**4 (blackbody radiation power vs temperature)
- Beer-Lambert law: I = c0 * exp(c1 * x) (light intensity attenuation through a medium)
- Michaelis-Menten kinetics: v = c0 * S / (S + c1) (enzyme-catalyzed reaction saturation)
- Hill equation: y = c0 * x**c1 / (x**c1 + c2) (cooperative binding, sigmoidal dose-response)
- Kepler's third law: T**2 = c0 * a**3 (orbital period vs semi-major axis)
- Newton's law of cooling: T = c0 + c1 * exp(c2 * t) (exponential thermal relaxation)
- Clausius-Clapeyron relation: log(P) = c0 + c1 / T (vapor pressure vs temperature)
- Langmuir adsorption isotherm: theta = c0 * P / (1 + c1 * P) (surface adsorption equilibrium)
- Freundlich isotherm: q = c0 * C**c1 (empirical adsorption on heterogeneous surface)
- Stokes' drag: F = c0 * r * v (viscous drag force on a sphere in fluid)
- Logistic growth: N = c0 / (1 + c1 * exp(c2 * t)) (population dynamics with carrying capacity)
- Planck-Wien approximation: I = c0 * f**3 * exp(c1 * f / T) (thermal radiation spectrum)
- Zero-order kinetics: dA_dt = -c0 (constant-rate consumption, e.g., saturated catalyst/constant feed removal)
- First-order kinetics: dA_dt = -c0 * A (unimolecular decay, radioactive/thermal decomposition, pseudo-first-order conditions)
- Second-order (self-reaction): dA_dt = -c0 * A**2 (bimolecular 2A -> products under mass action)
- General n-th order power-law: dA_dt = -c0 * A**c1 (empirical/global kinetic order when mechanism is unknown)
- Autocatalytic growth (logistic-type in A): dA_dt = c0 * A * (c1 - A) (self-catalysis with limiting capacity/inhibitory depletion approximated by c1 - A)
- Reversible first-order relaxation to equilibrium: dA_dt = -c0 * (A - c1) (approach to steady state/equilibrium concentration c1)
- Combined formation + decay: dA_dt = c0 - c1 * A (constant production with first-order loss; CSTR-like lumped dynamics)
- Rational-inhibition rate law: dA_dt = -c0 * A / (A + c1) (self-inhibition or limited availability modeled as a saturating effective rate)
- Rational activation (self-accelerating then limiting): dA_dt = -c0 * A**2 / (A + c1) (effective order transitions between 1st and 2nd order regimes)
- Time-dependent first-order rate coefficient: dA_dt = -(c0 + c1 * t) * A (linearly drifting rate due to changing conditions/temperature program folded into time)
- Exponentially deactivating kinetics: dA_dt = -c0 * exp(-c1 * t) * A (catalyst deactivation or quenched reactivity over time)
- Periodically forced kinetics: dA_dt = -(c0 + c1 * sin(c2 * t)) * A (periodic irradiation/mixing/temperature cycling affecting the effective rate)
- Stretched-exponential (time-varying hazard): dA_dt = -c0 * t**c1 * A (distributed processes/aging where the effective first-order rate scales as t**c1)

**Formula structure heuristic features**:
- Oscillation damping envelope → Exponential decay envelope f(x)*exp(-c*Abs(x)) for symmetric damped oscillation, Gaussian envelope f(x)*exp(-c*x**2) for localized wave packets
- Saturation/clipping effects → Rational fraction x/(1+x), tanh; for variables with alternating positive/negative in oscillatory systems, selectively apply Abs
- Growth/decay → Exponential growth exp(c*t), Logistic 1/(1+exp(-c*x)), power law x**c
- Threshold/activation behavior → Max(x-c, 0), piecewise functions
- Coupling/cross effects → Product terms between variables x*y, power-law coupling x**c1 * y**c2
- Mass-action signature: integer powers in A (A, A**2, A**3) suggest elementary unimolecular/bimolecular/termolecular steps or lumped approximations.
- Equilibrium/steady-state relaxation: a factor (A - c1) indicates convergence to a nonzero fixed point A = c1 rather than complete depletion.
- Source–sink balance: an additive constant term (c0) in dA_dt indicates feed/formation independent of A, typical of inflow, photogeneration at constant intensity, or zero-order formation.
- Catalyst deactivation / fading reactivity: a multiplicative time-decay factor exp(-c * t) multiplying A indicates the rate coefficient decreases with time rather than with concentration.
- Condition programming: explicit polynomial-in-t rate coefficients (c0 + c1*t + c2*t**2) indicate externally imposed ramps (temperature, light, mixing), not intrinsic chemistry in A alone.
- Mechanism change across regimes: rational forms like A/(A+c1) or A**2/(A+c1) encode smooth transitions between low-A and high-A kinetic orders.
- Self-accelerating vs self-limiting behavior: presence of both +A and -A**2 terms (e.g., A*(c1-A)) suggests autocatalysis tempered by depletion/inhibition.
- Identifiability caution: with only (t, A), different mechanisms can collapse to similar effective dA_dt(A,t); prefer minimal-order models unless residuals show structured time dependence.
- Physical feasibility constraints: for closed decay processes, enforce dA_dt <= 0 when A > 0 and avoid models that predict negative A unless additional species/balances justify it.

I need to analyze each candidate against the Ground Truth (GT):

**GT:** `-0.2092*A² + 0.2153*A²/(0.9716*A⁴ + 1) - 0.2092*A*exp(-0.0654*t)`

The GT has three terms:
1. A quadratic term: `c₀*A²`
2. A rational term: `A²/(a*A⁴ + 1)` — this is a ratio with A⁴ in the denominator
3. An exponential decay term: `A*exp(-b*t)`

Key structural features:
- The rational term `A²/(A⁴ + const)` cannot be simplified to simpler forms
- The exponential term couples A and t multiplicatively: `A*exp(c*t)`
- No constant offset term, no pure A term (linear), no log terms

Let me check each candidate systematically.

For a candidate to match, it must be able to produce:
1. An `A²` term
2. An `A²/(polynomial in A)` rational term (specifically A⁴ in denominator)
3. An `A*exp(t)` coupling term

Let me go through each candidate:

**Candidate 1:** `A²*c0 + A*c1 + A*c2 + A^c3*c4 + c5/(A+c6) + c7*exp(c8*t) + c9`
- Has `c5/(A+c6)` but GT needs `A²/(A⁴+1)` — these are structurally different rational functions
- Has `c7*exp(c8*t)` but GT needs `A*exp(t)` — missing the A multiplier
- Cannot match.
Candidate 1 verdict: [NO MATCH]

**Candidate 2:** `A²*c0 + A + c1*|A| + c2 + c3*exp(c4*t) + c5*exp(c6*t)*log(A*c7+1)`

- `c3*exp(c4*t)` — no A coupling, GT needs `A*exp(t)`
- `c5*exp(c6*t)*log(A*c7+1)` — this is exp(t)*log(A), not A*exp(t)
- Cannot produce `A²/(A⁴+1)` rational term
Candidate 2 verdict: [NO MATCH]
